<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сереть.html>сере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">serétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посереть.html>посере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poserétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сереть.html>сере́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become gray</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fade <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of talent</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to become commonplace</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посетовавший.html>посе́товавший</a> (19876)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посетить.html>посети́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">posetítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посещать.html>посеща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poseščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посетить.html>посети́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посеять.html>посе́ять</a> (12773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеять.html>се́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">séjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посеять.html>посе́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poséjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеять.html>се́ять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sow, to drill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose, to squander</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spread (an idea, fear etc.)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посидеть.html>посиде́ть</a> (2147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sidétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посидеть.html>посиде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posidétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sit (for a while)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:посидеть.html>посиди́м</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорожка.html>доро́жку</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Daváj <b>posidím</b> na doróžku.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Let's sit down for a bit before the road. (<i>a Russian tradition is to sit silently for a minute before a long journey</i>)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***поскользнуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поскользнуться.html>поскользну́ться</a> (12114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skolʹznútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поскользнуться.html>поскользну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poskolʹznútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поска́льзываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slip and fall, to especially on ice</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подскользну́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podskolʹznútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is much more common colloquially, but is often proscribed.</li></ul>

***поскольку.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поскольку.html>поско́льку</a> (737)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поскольку.html>поско́льку</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poskólʹku</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>inasmuch as, as</li>
<li>since
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поскольку.html>поско́льку</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:олимпийский.html>олимпи́йские</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>и́гры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собирать.html>собира́ют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сячи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болельщик.html>боле́льщиков</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спортсмен.html>спортсме́нов</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочить.html>со́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:построенный.html>постро́ены</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:десяток.html>деся́тки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гостиница.html>гости́ниц</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Poskólʹku</b> Olimpíjskije ígry sobirájut týsjači bolélʹščikov i sportsménov, v Sóči býli postrójeny desjátki nóvyx gostínic.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Since</b> the Olympic Games attract thousands of fans and athletes, dozens of new hotels were built in Sochi.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
